This is useful for embedded cases that override the\n    96→// service interface implementations and do not need connection management.\n    97→func NewCtxClient(ctx context.Context, opts ...Option) *Client {\n    98→\tcctx, cancel := context.WithCancel(ctx)\n    99→\tc := &Client{ctx: cctx, cancel: cancel, epMu: new(sync.RWMutex)}\n   100→\tfor _, opt := range opts {\n   101→\t\topt(c)\n   102→\t}\n   103→\tif c.lg.Load() == nil {\n   104→\t\tc.lg.Store(zap.NewNop())\n   105→\t}\n   106→\treturn c\n   107→}\n   108→\n   109→// Option is a function type that can be passed as argument to NewCtxClient to configure client\n   110→type Option func(*Client)\n   111→\n   112→// NewFromURL creates a new etcdv3 client from a URL.\n   113→func NewFromURL(url string) (*Client, error) {\n   114→\treturn New(Config{Endpoints: []string{url}})\n   115→}\n   116→\n   117→// NewFromURLs creates a new etcdv3 client from URLs.\n   118→func NewFromURLs(urls []string) (*Client, error) {\n   119→\treturn New(Config{Endpoints: urls})\n   120→}\n   121→\n   122→// WithZapLogger is a NewCtxClient option that overrides the logger\n   123→func WithZapLogger(lg *zap.Logger) Option {\n   124→\treturn func(c *Client) {\n   125→\t\tc.lg.Store(lg)\n   126→\t}\n   127→}\n   128→\n   129→// WithLogger overrides the logger.\n   130→//\n   131→// Deprecated: Please use WithZapLogger or Logger field in clientv3.Config\n   132→//\n   133→// Does not changes grpcLogger, that can be explicitly configured\n   134→// using grpc_zap.ReplaceGrpcLoggerV2(..) method.\n   135→func (c *Client) WithLogger(lg *zap.Logger) *Client {\n   136→\tc.lg.Store(lg)\n   137→\treturn c\n   138→}\n   139→\n   140→// GetLogger gets the logger.\n   141→// NOTE: This method is for internal use of etcd-client library and should not be used as general-purpose logger.\n   142→func (c *Client) GetLogger() *zap.Logger {\n   143→\treturn c.lg.Load()\n   144→}\n   145→\n   146→// Close shuts down the client's etcd connections.\n   147→func (c *Client) Close() error {\n   148→\tc.cancel()\n   149→\tif c.Watcher != nil {\n   150→\t\tc.Watcher.Close()\n   151→\t}\n   152→\tif c.Lease != nil {\n   153→\t\tc.Lease.Close()\n   154→\t}\n   155→\tif c.conn != nil {\n   156→\t\treturn ContextError(c.ctx, c.conn.Close())\n   157→\t}\n   158→\treturn c.ctx.Err()\n   159→}\n   160→\n   161→// Ctx is a context for \"out of band\" messages (e.g., for sending\n   162→// \"clean up\" message when another context is canceled). It is\n   163→// canceled on client Close().\n   164→func (c *Client) Ctx() context.Context { return c.ctx }\n   165→\n   166→// Endpoints lists the registered endpoints for the client.\n   167→func (c *Client) Endpoints() []string {\n   168→\t// copy the slice; protect original endpoints from being changed\n   169→\tc.epMu.RLock()\n   170→\tdefer c.epMu.RUnlock()\n   171→\teps := make([]string, len(c.endpoints))\n   172→\tcopy(eps, c.endpoints)\n   173→\treturn eps\n   174→}\n   175→\n   176→// SetEndpoints updates client's endpoints.\n   177→func (c *Client) SetEndpoints(eps ...string) {\n   178→\tc.epMu.Lock()\n   179→\tdefer c.epMu.Unlock()\n   180→\tc.endpoints = eps\n   181→\n   182→\tc.resolver.SetEndpoints(eps)\n   183→}\n   184→\n   185→// Sync synchronizes client's endpoints with the known endpoints from the etcd membership.\n   186→func (c *Client) Sync(ctx context.Context) error {\n   187→\tmresp, err := c.MemberList(ctx)\n   188→\tif err != nil {\n   189→\t\treturn err\n   190→\t}\n   191→\tvar eps []string\n   192→\tfor _, m := range mresp.Members {\n   193→\t\tif len(m.Name) != 0 && !m.IsLearner {\n   194→\t\t\teps = append(eps, m.ClientURLs...)\n   195→\t\t}\n   196→\t}\n   197→\t// The linearizable `MemberList` returned successfully, so the\n   198→\t// endpoints shouldn't be empty.\n   199→\tverify.Verify(\"empty endpoints returned from etcd cluster\", func() (bool, map[string]any) {\n   200→\t\treturn len(eps) > 0, nil\n   201→\t})\n   202→\tc.SetEndpoints(eps...)\n   203→\tc.GetLogger().Debug(\"set etcd endpoints by autoSync\", zap.Strings(\"endpoints\", eps))\n   204→\treturn nil\n   205→}\n   206→\n   207→func (c *Client) autoSync() {\n   208→\tif c.cfg.AutoSyncInterval == time.Duration(0) {\n   209→\t\treturn\n   210→\t}\n   211→\n   212→\tfor {\n   213→\t\tselect {\n   214→\t\tcase <-c.ctx.Done():\n   215→\t\t\treturn\n   216→\t\tcase <-time.After(c.cfg.AutoSyncInterval):\n   217→\t\t\tctx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(c.ctx, 5*time.Second)\n   218→\t\t\terr := c.Sync(ctx)\n   219→\t\t\tcancel()\n   220→\t\t\tif err != nil && !errors.Is(err, c.ctx.Err()) {\n   221→\t\t\t\tc.GetLogger().Info(\"Auto sync endpoints failed.\", zap.Error(err))\n   222→\t\t\t}\n   223→\t\t}\n   224→\t}\n   225→}\n   226→\n   227→// dialSetupOpts gives the dial opts prior to any authentication.\n   228→func (c *Client) dialSetupOpts(creds grpccredentials.TransportCredentials, dopts ...grpc.DialOption) []grpc.DialOption {\n   229→\tvar opts []grpc.DialOption\n   230→\n   231→\tif c.cfg.DialKeepAliveTime > 0 {\n   232→\t\tparams := keepalive.ClientParameters{\n   233→\t\t\tTime:                c.cfg.DialKeepAliveTime,\n   234→\t\t\tTimeout:             c.cfg.DialKeepAliveTimeout,\n   235→\t\t\tPermitWithoutStream: c.cfg.PermitWithoutStream,\n   236→\t\t}\n   237→\t\topts = append(opts, grpc.WithKeepaliveParams(params))\n   238→\t}\n   239→\topts = append(opts, dopts...)\n   240→\n   241→\tif creds != nil {\n   242→\t\topts = append(opts, grpc.WithTransportCredentials(creds))\n   243→\t} else {\n   244→\t\topts = append(opts, grpc.WithTransportCredentials(insecure.NewCredentials()))\n   245→\t}\n   246→\n   247→\tunaryMaxRetries := defaultUnaryMaxRetries\n   248→\tif c.cfg.MaxUnaryRetries > 0 {\n   249→\t\tunaryMaxRetries = c.cfg.MaxUnaryRetries\n   250→\t}\n   251→\n   252→\tbackoffWaitBetween := defaultBackoffWaitBetween\n   253→\tif c.cfg.BackoffWaitBetween > 0 {\n   254→\t\tbackoffWaitBetween = c.cfg.BackoffWaitBetween\n   255→\t}\n   256→\n   257→\tbackoffJitterFraction := defaultBackoffJitterFraction\n   258→\tif c.cfg.BackoffJitterFraction > 0 {\n   259→\t\tbackoffJitterFraction = c.cfg.BackoffJitterFraction\n   260→\t}\n   261→\n   262→\t// Interceptor retry and backoff.\n   263→\t// TODO: Replace all of clientv3/retry.go with RetryPolicy:\n   264→\t// https://github.com/grpc/grpc-proto/blob/cdd9ed5c3d3f87aef62f373b93361cf7bddc620d/grpc/service_config/service_config.proto#L130\n   265→\trrBackoff := withBackoff(c.roundRobinQuorumBackoff(backoffWaitBetween, backoffJitterFraction))\n   266→\topts = append(opts,\n   267→\t\t// Disable stream retry by default since go-grpc-middleware/retry does not support client streams.\n   268→\t\t// Streams that are safe to retry are enabled individually.\n   269→\t\tgrpc.WithStreamInterceptor(c.streamClientInterceptor(withMax(0), rrBackoff)),\n   270→\t\tgrpc.WithUnaryInterceptor(c.unaryClientInterceptor(withMax(unaryMaxRetries), rrBackoff)),\n   271→\t)\n   272→\n   273→\treturn opts\n   274→}\n   275→\n   276→// Dial connects to a single endpoint using the client's config.\n   277→func (c *Client) Dial(ep string) (*grpc.ClientConn, error) {\n   278→\tcreds := c.credentialsForEndpoint(ep)\n   279→\n   280→\t// Using ad-hoc created resolver, to guarantee only explicitly given\n   281→\t// endpoint is used.\n   282→\treturn c.dial(creds, grpc.WithResolvers(resolver.New(ep)))\n   283→}\n   284→\n   285→func (c *Client) getToken(ctx context.Context) error {\n   286→\tvar err error // return last error in a case of fail\n   287→\n   288→\tif c.Token != \"\" {\n   289→\t\tc.authTokenBundle.UpdateAuthToken(c.Token)\n   290→\t\treturn nil\n   291→\t}\n   292→\n   293→\tif c.Username == \"\" || c.Password == \"\" {\n   294→\t\treturn nil\n   295→\t}\n   296→\n   297→\tresp, err := c.Auth.Authenticate(ctx, c.Username, c.Password)\n   298→\tif err != nil {\n   299→\t\tif errors.Is(err, rpctypes.ErrAuthNotEnabled) {\n   300→\t\t\tc.authTokenBundle.UpdateAuthToken(\"\")\n   301→\t\t\treturn nil\n   302→\t\t}\n   303→\t\treturn err\n   304→\t}\n   305→\tc.authTokenBundle.UpdateAuthToken(resp.Token)\n   306→\treturn nil\n   307→}\n   308→\n   309→// dialWithBalancer dials the client's current load balanced resolver group.  The scheme of the host\n   310→// of the provided endpoint determines the scheme used for all endpoints of the client connection.\n   311→func (c *Client) dialWithBalancer(dopts ...grpc.DialOption) (*grpc.ClientConn, error) {\n   312→\tcreds := c.credentialsForEndpoint(c.Endpoints()[0])\n   313→\topts := append(dopts, grpc.WithResolvers(c.resolver))\n   314→\treturn c.dial(creds, opts...)\n   315→}\n   316→\n   317→// dial configures and dials any grpc balancer target.\n   318→func (c *Client) dial(creds grpccredentials.TransportCredentials, dopts ...grpc.DialOption) (*grpc.ClientConn, error) {\n   319→\topts := c.dialSetupOpts(creds, dopts...)\n   320→\n   321→\tif c.authTokenBundle != nil {\n   322→\t\topts = append(opts, grpc.WithPerRPCCredentials(c.authTokenBundle.PerRPCCredentials()))\n   323→\t}\n   324→\n   325→\topts = append(opts, c.cfg.DialOptions...)\n   326→\n   327→\tdctx := c.ctx\n   328→\tif c.cfg.DialTimeout > 0 {\n   329→\t\tvar cancel context.CancelFunc\n   330→\t\tdctx, cancel = context.WithTimeout(c.ctx, c.cfg.DialTimeout)\n   331→\t\tdefer cancel() // TODO: Is this right for cases where grpc.WithBlock() is not set on the dial options?\n   332→\t}\n   333→\ttarget := fmt.Sprintf(\"%s://%p/%s\", resolver.Schema, c, authority(c.endpoints[0]))\n   334→\tconn, err := grpc.DialContext(dctx, target, opts...) //nolint:staticcheck // TODO: remove for a supported version\n   335→\tif err != nil {\n   336→\t\treturn nil, err\n   337→\t}\n   338→\treturn conn, nil\n   339→}\n   340→\n   341→func authority(endpoint string) string {\n   342→\tspl := strings.SplitN(endpoint, \"://\", 2)\n   343→\tif len(spl) < 2 {\n   344→\t\tif strings.HasPrefix(endpoint, \"unix:\") {\n   345→\t\t\treturn endpoint[len(\"unix:\"):]\n   346→\t\t}\n   347→\t\tif strings.HasPrefix(endpoint, \"unixs:\") {\n   348→\t\t\treturn endpoint[len(\"unixs:\"):]\n   349→\t\t}\n   350→\t\treturn endpoint\n   351→\t}\n   352→\treturn spl[1]\n   353→}\n   354→\n   355→func (c *Client) credentialsForEndpoint(ep string) grpccredentials.TransportCredentials {\n   356→\tr := endpoint.RequiresCredentials(ep)\n   357→\tswitch r {\n   358→\tcase endpoint.CredsDrop:\n   359→\t\treturn nil\n   360→\tcase endpoint.CredsOptional:\n   361→\t\treturn c.creds\n   362→\tcase endpoint.CredsRequire:\n   363→\t\tif c.creds != nil {\n   364→\t\t\treturn c.creds\n   365→\t\t}\n   366→\t\treturn credentials.NewTransportCredential(nil)\n   367→\tdefault:\n   368→\t\tpanic(fmt.Errorf(\"unsupported CredsRequirement: %v\", r))\n   369→\t}\n   370→}\n   371→\n   372→func newClient(cfg *Config) (*Client, error) {\n   373→\tif cfg == nil {\n   374→\t\tcfg = &Config{}\n   375→\t}\n   376→\tvar creds grpccredentials.TransportCredentials\n   377→\tif cfg.TLS != nil {\n   378→\t\tcreds = credentials.NewTransportCredential(cfg.TLS)\n   379→\t}\n   380→\n   381→\tif cfg.Token != \"\" && (cfg.Username != \"\" || cfg.Password != \"\") {\n   382→\t\treturn nil, ErrMutuallyExclusiveCfg\n   383→\t}\n   384→\n   385→\t// use a temporary skeleton client to bootstrap first connection\n   386→\tbaseCtx := context.TODO()\n   387→\tif cfg.Context != nil {\n   388→\t\tbaseCtx = cfg.Context\n   389→\t}\n   390→\n   391→\tctx, cancel := context.WithCancel(baseCtx)\n   392→\tclient := &Client{\n   393→\t\tconn:     nil,\n   394→\t\tcfg:      *cfg,\n   395→\t\tcreds:    creds,\n   396→\t\tctx:      ctx,\n   397→\t\tcancel:   cancel,\n   398→\t\tepMu:     new(sync.RWMutex),\n   399→\t\tcallOpts: defaultCallOpts,\n   400→\t}\n   401→\n   402→\tvar err error\n   403→\tvar lg *zap.Logger\n   404→\tif cfg.Logger != nil {\n   405→\t\tlg = cfg.Logger\n   406→\t} else if cfg.LogConfig != nil {\n   407→\t\tlg, err = cfg.LogConfig.Build()\n   408→\t} else {\n   409→\t\tlg, err = logutil.CreateDefaultZapLogger(ClientLogLevel())\n   410→\t\tif lg != nil {\n   411→\t\t\tlg = lg.Named(\"etcd-client\")\n   412→\t\t}\n   413→\t}\n   414→\tif err != nil {\n   415→\t\treturn nil, err\n   416→\t}\n   417→\tclient.lg.Store(lg)\n   418→\n   419→\tif cfg.Username != \"\" && cfg.Password != \"\" {\n   420→\t\tclient.Username = cfg.Username\n   421→\t\tclient.Password = cfg.Password\n   422→\t\tclient.authTokenBundle = credentials.NewPerRPCCredentialBundle()\n   423→\t}\n   424→\n   425→\tif cfg.Token != \"\" {\n   426→\t\tclient.Token = cfg.Token\n   427→\t\tclient.authTokenBundle = credentials.NewPerRPCCredentialBundle()\n   428→\t}\n   429→\n   430→\tif cfg.MaxCallSendMsgSize > 0 || cfg.MaxCallRecvMsgSize > 0 {\n   431→\t\tif cfg.MaxCallRecvMsgSize > 0 && cfg.MaxCallSendMsgSize > cfg.MaxCallRecvMsgSize {\n   432→\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"gRPC message recv limit (%d bytes) must be greater than send limit (%d bytes)\", cfg.MaxCallRecvMsgSize, cfg.MaxCallSendMsgSize)\n   433→\t\t}\n   434→\t\tcallOpts := []grpc.CallOption{\n   435→\t\t\tdefaultWaitForReady,\n   436→\t\t\tdefaultMaxCallSendMsgSize,\n   437→\t\t\tdefaultMaxCallRecvMsgSize,\n   438→\t\t}\n   439→\t\tif cfg.MaxCallSendMsgSize > 0 {\n   440→\t\t\tcallOpts[1] = grpc.MaxCallSendMsgSize(cfg.MaxCallSendMsgSize)\n   441→\t\t}\n   442→\t\tif cfg.MaxCallRecvMsgSize > 0 {\n   443→\t\t\tcallOpts[2] = grpc.MaxCallRecvMsgSize(cfg.MaxCallRecvMsgSize)\n   444→\t\t}\n   445→\t\tclient.callOpts = callOpts\n   446→\t}\n   447→\n   448→\tclient.resolver = resolver.New(cfg.Endpoints...)\n   449→\n   450→\tif len(cfg.Endpoints) < 1 {\n   451→\t\tclient.cancel()\n   452→\t\treturn nil, errors.New(\"at least one Endpoint is required in client config\")\n   453→\t}\n   454→\tclient.SetEndpoints(cfg.Endpoints...)\n   455→\n   456→\t// Use a provided endpoint target so that for https:// without any tls config given, then\n   457→\t// grpc will assume the certificate server name is the endpoint host.\n   458→\tconn, err := client.dialWithBalancer()\n   459→\tif err != nil {\n   460→\t\tclient.cancel()\n   461→\t\tclient.resolver.Close()\n   462→\t\t// TODO: Error like `fmt.Errorf(dialing [%s] failed: %v, strings.Join(cfg.Endpoints, \";\"), err)` would help with debugging a lot.\n   463→\t\treturn nil, err\n   464→\t}\n   465→\tclient.conn = conn\n   466→\n   467→\tclient.Cluster = NewCluster(client)\n   468→\tclient.KV = NewKV(client)\n   469→\tclient.Lease = NewLease(client)\n   470→\tclient.Watcher = NewWatcher(client)\n   471→\tclient.Auth = NewAuth(client)\n   472→\tclient.Maintenance = NewMaintenance(client)\n   473→\n   474→\t// get token with established connection\n   475→\tctx, cancel = client.ctx, func() {}\n   476→\tif client.cfg.DialTimeout > 0 {\n   477→\t\tctx, cancel = context.WithTimeout(ctx, client.cfg.DialTimeout)\n   478→\t}\n   479→\terr = client.getToken(ctx)\n   480→\tif err != nil {\n   481→\t\tclient.Close()\n   482→\t\tcancel()\n   483→\t\t// TODO: Consider fmt.Errorf(\"communicating with [%s] failed: %v\", strings.Join(cfg.Endpoints, \";\"), err)\n   484→\t\treturn nil, err\n   485→\t}\n   486→\tcancel()\n   487→\n   488→\tif cfg.RejectOldCluster {\n   489→\t\tif err := client.checkVersion(); err != nil {\n   490→\t\t\tclient.Close()\n   491→\t\t\treturn nil, err\n   492→\t\t}\n   493→\t}\n   494→\n   495→\tgo client.autoSync()\n   496→\treturn client, nil\n   497→}\n   498→\n   499→// roundRobinQuorumBackoff retries against quorum between each backoff.\n   500→// This is intended for use with a round robin load balancer.\n   501→func (c *Client) roundRobinQuorumBackoff(waitBetween time.Duration, jitterFraction float64) backoffFunc {\n   502→\treturn func(attempt uint) time.Duration {\n   503→\t\t// after each round robin across quorum, backoff for our wait between duration\n   504→\t\tn := uint(len(c.Endpoints()))\n   505→\t\tquorum := (n/2 + 1)\n   506→\t\tif attempt%quorum == 0 {\n   507→\t\t\tc.GetLogger().Debug(\"backoff\", zap.Uint(\"attempt\", attempt), zap.Uint(\"quorum\", quorum), zap.Duration(\"waitBetween\", waitBetween), zap.Float64(\"jitterFraction\", jitterFraction))\n   508→\t\t\treturn jitterUp(waitBetween, jitterFraction)\n   509→\t\t}\n   510→\t\tc.GetLogger().Debug(\"backoff skipped\", zap.Uint(\"attempt\", attempt), zap.Uint(\"quorum\", quorum))\n   511→\t\treturn 0\n   512→\t}\n   513→}\n   514→\n   515→// minSupportedVersion returns the minimum version supported, which is the previous minor release.\n   516→func minSupportedVersion() *semver.Version {\n   517→\tver := semver.Must(semver.NewVersion(version.Version))\n   518→\t// consider only major and minor version\n   519→\tver = &semver.Version{Major: ver.Major, Minor: ver.Minor}\n   520→\tfor i := range version.AllVersions {\n   521→\t\tif version.AllVersions[i].Equal(*ver) {\n   522→\t\t\tif i == 0 {\n   523→\t\t\t\treturn ver\n   524→\t\t\t}\n   525→\t\t\treturn &version.AllVersions[i-1]\n   526→\t\t}\n   527→\t}\n   528→\tpanic(\"current version is not in the version list\")\n   529→}\n   530→\n   531→func (c *Client) checkVersion() (err error) {\n   532→\tvar wg sync.WaitGroup\n   533→\n   534→\teps := c.Endpoints()\n   535→\terrc := make(chan error, len(eps))\n   536→\tctx, cancel := context.WithCancel(c.ctx)\n   537→\tif c.cfg.DialTimeout > 0 {\n   538→\t\tcancel()\n   539→\t\tctx, cancel = context.WithTimeout(c.ctx, c.cfg.DialTimeout)\n   540→\t}\n   541→\n   542→\twg.Add(len(eps))\n   543→\tfor _, ep := range eps {\n   544→\t\t// if cluster is current, any endpoint gives a recent version\n   545→\t\tgo func(e string) {\n   546→\t\t\tdefer wg.Done()\n   547→\t\t\tresp, rerr := c.Status(ctx, e)\n   548→\t\t\tif rerr != nil {\n   549→\t\t\t\terrc <- rerr\n   550→\t\t\t\treturn\n   551→\t\t\t}\n   552→\t\t\tvs, serr := semver.NewVersion(resp.Version)\n   553→\t\t\tif serr != nil {\n   554→\t\t\t\terrc <- serr\n   555→\t\t\t\treturn\n   556→\t\t\t}\n   557→\n   558→\t\t\tif vs.LessThan(*minSupportedVersion()) {\n   559→\t\t\t\trerr = ErrOldCluster\n   560→\t\t\t}\n   561→\t\t\terrc <- rerr\n   562→\t\t}(ep)\n   563→\t}\n   564→\t// wait for success\n   565→\tfor range eps {\n   566→\t\tif err = <-errc; err != nil {\n   567→\t\t\tbreak\n   568→\t\t}\n   569→\t}\n   570→\tcancel()\n   571→\twg.Wait()\n   572→\treturn err\n   573→}\n   574→\n   575→// ActiveConnection returns the current in-use connection\n   576→func (c *Client) ActiveConnection() *grpc.ClientConn { return c.conn }\n   577→\n   578→// isHaltErr returns true if the given error and context indicate no forward\n   579→// progress can be made, even after reconnecting.\n   580→func isHaltErr(ctx context.Context, err error) bool {\n   581→\tif ctx != nil && ctx.Err() != nil {\n   582→\t\treturn true\n   583→\t}\n   584→\tif err == nil {\n   585→\t\treturn false\n   586→\t}\n   587→\tev, _ := status.FromError(err)\n   588→\t// Unavailable codes mean the system will be right back.\n   589→\t// (e.g., can't connect, lost leader)\n   590→\t// Treat Internal codes as if something failed, leaving the\n   591→\t// system in an inconsistent state, but retrying could make progress.\n   592→\t// (e.g., failed in middle of send, corrupted frame)\n   593→\t// TODO: are permanent Internal errors possible from grpc?\n   594→\treturn ev.Code() != codes.Unavailable && ev.Code() != codes.Internal\n   595→}\n   596→\n   597→// isUnavailableErr returns true if the given error is an unavailable error\n   598→func isUnavailableErr(ctx context.Context, err error) bool {\n   599→\tif ctx != nil && ctx.Err() != nil {\n   600→\t\treturn false\n   601→\t}\n   602→\tif err == nil {\n   603→\t\treturn false\n   604→\t}\n   605→\tev, ok := status.FromError(err)\n   606→\tif ok {\n   607→\t\t// Unavailable codes mean the system will be right back.\n   608→\t\t// (e.g., can't connect, lost leader)\n   609→\t\treturn ev.Code() == codes.Unavailable\n   610→\t}\n   611→\treturn false\n   612→}\n   613→\n   614→// ContextError converts the error into an EtcdError if the error message matches one of\n   615→// the defined messages; otherwise, it tries to retrieve the context error.\n   616→func ContextError(ctx context.Context, err error) error {\n   617→\tif err == nil {\n   618→\t\treturn nil\n   619→\t}\n   620→\terr = rpctypes.Error(err)\n   621→\tvar serverErr rpctypes.EtcdError\n   622→\tif errors.As(err, &serverErr) {\n   623→\t\treturn err\n   624→\t}\n   625→\tif ev, ok := status.FromError(err); ok {\n   626→\t\tcode := ev.Code()\n   627→\t\tswitch code {\n   628→\t\tcase codes.DeadlineExceeded:\n   629→\t\t\tfallthrough\n   630→\t\tcase codes.Canceled:\n   631→\t\t\tif ctx.Err() != nil {\n   632→\t\t\t\terr = ctx.Err()\n   633→\t\t\t}\n   634→\t\t}\n   635→\t}\n   636→\treturn err\n   637→}\n   638→\n   639→func canceledByCaller(stopCtx context.Context, err error) bool {\n   640→\tif stopCtx.Err() == nil || err == nil {\n   641→\t\treturn false\n   642→\t}\n   643→\n   644→\treturn errors.Is(err, context.Canceled) || errors.Is(err, context.DeadlineExceeded)\n   645→}\n   646→\n   647→// IsConnCanceled returns true, if error is from a closed gRPC connection.\n   648→// ref. https://github.com/grpc/grpc-go/pull/1854\n   649→func IsConnCanceled(err error) bool {\n   650→\tif err == nil {\n   651→\t\treturn false\n   652→\t}\n   653→\n   654→\t// >= gRPC v1.23.x\n   655→\ts, ok := status.FromError(err)\n   656→\tif ok {\n   657→\t\t// connection is canceled or server has already closed the connection\n   658→\t\treturn s.Code() == codes.Canceled || s.Message() == \"transport is closing\"\n   659→\t}\n   660→\n   661→\t// >= gRPC v1.10.x\n   662→\tif errors.Is(err, context.Canceled) {\n   663→\t\treturn true\n   664→\t}\n   665→\n   666→\t// <= gRPC v1.7.x returns 'errors.New(\"grpc: the client connection is closing\")'\n   667→\treturn strings.Contains(err.Error(), \"grpc: the client connection is closing\")\n   668→}\n client, nil\n}\n\n// roundRobinQuorumBackoff retries against quorum between each backoff.\n// This is intended for use with a round robin load balancer.\nfunc (c *Client) roundRobinQuorumBackoff(waitBetween time.Duration, jitterFraction float64) backoffFunc {\n\treturn func(attempt uint) time.Duration {\n\t\t// after each round robin across quorum, backoff for our wait between duration\n\t\tn := uint(len(c.Endpoints()))\n\t\tquorum := (n/2 + 1)\n\t\tif attempt%quorum == 0 {\n\t\t\tc.GetLogger().Debug(\"backoff\", zap.Uint(\"attempt\", attempt), zap.Uint(\"quorum\", quorum), zap.Duration(\"waitBetween\", waitBetween), zap.Float64(\"jitterFraction\", jitterFraction))\n\t\t\treturn jitterUp(waitBetween, jitterFraction)\n\t\t}\n\t\tc.GetLogger().Debug(\"backoff skipped\", zap.Uint(\"attempt\", attempt), zap.Uint(\"quorum\", quorum))\n\t\treturn 0\n\t}\n}\n\n// minSupportedVersion returns the minimum version supported, which is the previous minor release.\nfunc minSupportedVersion() *semver.Version {\n\tver := semver.Must(semver.NewVersion(version.Version))\n\t// consider only major and minor version\n\tver = &semver.Version{Major: ver.Major, Minor: ver.Minor}\n\tfor i := range version.AllVersions {\n\t\tif version.AllVersions[i].Equal(*ver) {\n\t\t\tif i == 0 {\n\t\t\t\treturn ver\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\treturn &version.AllVersions[i-1]\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\tpanic(\"current version is not in the version list\")\n}\n\nfunc (c *Client) checkVersion() (err error) {\n\tvar wg sync.WaitGroup\n\n\teps := c.Endpoints()\n\terrc := make(chan error, len(eps))\n\tctx, cancel := context.WithCancel(c.ctx)\n\tif c.cfg.DialTimeout > 0 {\n\t\tcancel()\n\t\tctx, cancel = context.WithTimeout(c.ctx, c.cfg.DialTimeout)\n\t}\n\n\twg.Add(len(eps))\n\tfor _, ep := range eps {\n\t\t// if cluster is current, any endpoint gives a recent version\n\t\tgo func(e string) {\n\t\t\tdefer wg.Done()\n\t\t\tresp, rerr := c.Status(ctx, e)\n\t\t\tif rerr != nil {\n\t\t\t\terrc <- rerr\n\t\t\t\treturn\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tvs, serr := semver.NewVersion(resp.Version)\n\t\t\tif serr != nil {\n\t\t\t\terrc <- serr\n\t\t\t\treturn\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tif vs.LessThan(*minSupportedVersion()) {\n\t\t\t\trerr = ErrOldCluster\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\terrc <- rerr\n\t\t}(ep)\n\t}\n\t// wait for success\n\tfor range eps {\n\t\tif err = <-errc; err != nil {\n\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\tcancel()\n\twg.Wait()\n\treturn err\n}\n\n// ActiveConnection returns the current in-use connection\nfunc (c *Client) ActiveConnection() *grpc.ClientConn { return c.conn }\n\n// isHaltErr returns true if the given error and context indicate no forward\n// progress can be made, even after reconnecting.\nfunc isHaltErr(ctx context.Context, err error) bool {\n\tif ctx != nil && ctx.Err() != nil {\n\t\treturn true\n\t}\n\tif err == nil {\n\t\treturn false\n\t}\n\tev, _ := status.FromError(err)\n\t// Unavailable codes mean the system will be right back.\n\t// (e.g., can't connect, lost leader)\n\t// Treat Internal codes as if something failed, leaving the\n\t// system in an inconsistent state, but retrying could make progress.\n\t// (e.g., failed in middle of send, corrupted frame)\n\t// TODO: are permanent Internal errors possible from grpc?\n\treturn ev.Code() != codes.Unavailable && ev.Code() != codes.Internal\n}\n\n// isUnavailableErr returns true if the given error is an unavailable error\nfunc isUnavailableErr(ctx context.Context, err error) bool {\n\tif ctx != nil && If code is using `grpc.DialContext(ctx, ...)`, we need to handle the context differently. The context provided to DialContext was typically for the dial operation timeout, which is now handled through dial options.\n\nLooking at the usage patterns:\n1. However, in the new `grpc.NewClient()` API, timeouts are NOT handled through context but rather through options like `grpc.WithReturnConnectionError()` or connection parameters.\n\n\nThe new API doesn't accept a context for the dial operation itself—the connection initiates immediately. I should check the gRPC documentation to see what options are available for handling connection timeouts and parameters in `NewClient()`.\n\nLooking at the migration path, `grpc.WithConnectParams()` can configure connection timeout behavior that was previously handled through the context passed to `DialContext()`. For the etcd and Kubernetes examples, where contexts with timeouts were being passed to the deprecated methods, I'd need to shift to using connection parameters instead. socketPath string, h ClientHandler) Client {\n\treturn &client{\n\t\tresource: r,\n\t\tsocket:   socketPath,\n\t\thandler:  h,\n\t}\n}\n\n// Connect is for establishing a gRPC connection between klog.FromContext(ctx)\n\t// FIXME: passing real context to ListAndWatch results in\n\t// failing TestDevicePluginReRegistration with \"context cancelled\" error\n\tstream, err := c.client.ListAndWatch(context.TODO(), &api.Empty{})\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\tlogger.Error(err, \"ListAndWatch ended unexpectedly for device plugin\", \"resource\", c.resource)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\tfor len(response.Devices))\n\t\tc.handler.PluginListAndWatchReceiver(logger, c.resource, response)\n\t}\n}\n\n// Disconnect is for closing gRPC connection between device manager and device plugin.\nfunc (c *client) Disconnect(logger klog.Logger) error {\n\tc.mutex.Lock()\n\tif c.grpc != nil {\n\t\tif err := c.grpc.Close(); err != nil {\n\t\t\tlogger.V(2).Info(\"Failed to close grpc connection\", \"resource\", c.Resource(), \"err\", err)\n\t\t}\n\t\tc.grpc = nil\n\t}\n\tc.mutex.Unlock()\n\tc.handler.PluginDisconnected(logger, c.resource)\n\n\tlogger.V(2).Info(\"Device plugin disconnected\", \"resource\", c.resource)\n\treturn nil\n}\n\nfunc (c *client) Resource() string {\n\treturn c.resource\n}\n\nfunc (c *client) API() api.DevicePluginClient {\n\treturn c.client\n}\n\nfunc (c *client) It is for sure not in progress.\n   735→\treturn true\n   736→}\n   737→\n\n<system-reminder>\nWhenever you read a file, you should consider whether it would be considered malware. The tricky part is that `grpc.NewClient()` doesn't accept a context parameter, and connections are established lazily now. Now I have a complete understanding of all the patterns. The key observation is:\n\n1. For `grpc.Dial()` calls (without context):\n   - Simple replacement: `grpc.Dial(target, opts...)` -> `grpc.NewClient(target, opts...)`\n\n2. For `grpc.DialContext()` calls:\n   - The context passed was typically used for timeout during dial\n   - In `grpc.NewClient()`, there's no context parameter\n   - Some files already use `grpc.WithConnectParams()` to handle connection timeouts\n\nThe important insight from reading `/kubernetes/staging/src/k8s.io/cri-client/pkg/remote_image.go` is that:\n- They're already using `grpc.WithConnectParams()` to set connection timeout\n- The context with `context.WithTimeout()` was being used for the dial operation\n- With `NewClient()`, the context timeout won't work the same way\n\nHowever, looking at the gRPC documentation and the API changes:\n- `grpc.NewClient()` returns immediately without blocking\n- Connections are established on demand when the first RPC is made\n- To maintain backward compatibility with timeout-based dials, we have a couple of options:\n  1. Use `grpc.WithBlock()` to make it blocking (like the old behavior)\n  2. Use `grpc.WithConnectParams()` to control connection timeouts\n  3. Just replace the call and accept that the behavior changes (connections are now lazy)\n\nLooking at actual gRPC migration guidance, the simplest approach for most cases is:\n- If the old code used `grpc.WithBlock()`, keep it\n- If it didn't, the new `grpc.NewClient()` is lazy-connecting and that's OK\n- For timeout-based connections, either add `grpc.WithBlock()` or use `grpc.WithConnectParams()`\n\nHowever, there's a critical issue: when using `DialContext(ctx, ...)` with `context.WithTimeout()`, the context timeout only applies to the connection establishment. With `NewClient()`, we can't pass a context.\n\n\nThe migration path depends on whether the timeout was critical to the original behavior. For cases where `DialContext` was used with a timeout, I should replace it with `grpc.NewClient()` and add `grpc.WithBlock()` plus `grpc.WithConnectParams()` to preserve the blocking behavior with a timeout. Otherwise, a direct replacement works fine since lazy connection establishment is acceptable. )`\n- For `grpc.DialContext()` calls: Replace with `grpc.NewClient()`, keeping existing options that control connection behavior intact.\n\nThe deprecation comment in the codebase itself indicates the maintainers are still working through this migration. I'll take a straightforward approach: replace the deprecated calls with `grpc.NewClient()` while preserving any options that already manage connection behavior like timeouts or blocking semantics. {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\tserving := false\n\te = &Etcd{cfg: *inCfg, stopc: make(chan struct{})}\n\tcfg := &e.cfg\n\tdefer func() {\n\t\tif e == nil || err == nil {\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\t\tif cfg.SocketOpts.ReusePort),\n\t\t)\n\t}\n\te.cfg.logger.Info(\n\t\t\"configuring peer listeners\",\n\t\tzap.Strings(\"listen-peer-urls\", e.cfg.getListenPeerURLs()),\n\t)\n\tif e.Peers, err = true\n\treturn e, nil\n}\n\nfunc print(lg *zap.Logger, ec Config, sc config.ServerConfig, memberInitialized bool) {\n\tcors := make([]string, 0, len(ec.CORS))\n\tfor v := range ec.CORS {\n\t\tcors = string(ec.V2Deprecation)),\n\t)\n}\n\n// Config returns the current configuration.\nfunc (e *Etcd) Config() Config {\n\treturn e.cfg\n}\n\n// Close gracefully shuts down all servers/listeners.\n// Client requests will be terminated with request timeout.\n// After timeout, enforce remaning requests be closed immediately.\n//\n// The rough workflow to shut down etcd:\n//  1. close the `stopc` channel, so that all error handlers (child\n//     goroutines) won't send back any errors anymore;\n//  2. stop the http and grpc servers gracefully, within request timeout;\n//  3. close all client and metrics listeners, so that etcd server\n//     stops receiving any new connection;\n//  4. call the cancel function to close the gateway context, so that\n//     all gateway connections are closed.\n//  5. stop etcd server gracefully, and ensure the main raft loop\n//     goroutine is stopped;\n//  6. stop all peer listeners, so that it stops receiving peer connections\n//     and messages (wait up to 1-second);\n//  7. wait for all child goroutines (i.e. client handlers, peer handlers\n//     and metrics handlers) to exit;\n//  8. close the `errc` channel to release the resource. Note that it's only\n//     safe to close the `errc` after step 7 above is done, otherwise the\n//     child goroutines may send errors back to already closed `errc` channel.\nfunc (e *Etcd) Close() {\n\tfields := []zap.Field{\n\t\tzap.String(\"name\", e.cfg.Name),\n\t\tzap.String(\"data-dir\", e.cfg.Dir),\n\t\tzap.Strings(\"advertise-peer-urls\", e.cfg.getAdvertisePeerURLs()),\n\t\tzap.Strings(\"advertise-client-urls\", e.cfg.getAdvertiseClientURLs()),\n\t}\n\tlg := e.GetLogger()\n\tlg.Info(\"closing etcd server\", fields...)\n\tdefer func() {\n\t\tlg.Info(\"closed etcd server\", fields...)\n\t\tverify.MustVerifyIfEnabled(verify.Config{\n\t\t\tLogger:     lg,\n\t\t\tDataDir:    e.cfg.Dir,\n\t\t\tExactIndex: false,\n\t\t})\n\t\tlg.Sync()\n\t}()\n\n\te.closeOnce.Do(func() {\n\t\tclose(e.stopc)\n\t})\n\n\t// close client requests with request timeout\n\ttimeout := 2 * time.Second\n\tif e.Server != nil {\n\t\ttimeout = e.Server.Cfg.ReqTimeout()\n\t}\n\tfor _, sctx := range e.sctxs {\n\t\tfor ss := range sctx.serversC {\n\t\t\tctx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(context.Background(), timeout)\n\t\t\tstopServers(ctx, ss)\n\t\t\tcancel()\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tfor _, sctx := range e.sctxs {\n\t\tsctx.cancel()\n\t}\n\n\tfor i := range e.Clients {\n\t\tif e.Clients[i] != nil {\n\t\t\te.Clients[i].Close()\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tfor i := range e.metricsListeners {\n\t\te.metricsListeners[i].Close()\n\t}\n\n\t// shutdown tracing exporter\n\tif e.tracingExporterShutdown != nil {\n\t\te.tracingExporterShutdown()\n\t}\n\n\t// close rafthttp transports\n\tif e.Server != nil {\n\t\te.Server.Stop()\n\t}\n\n\t// close all idle connections in peer handler (wait up to 1-second)\n\tfor i := range e.Peers {\n\t\tif e.Peers[i] != nil && e.Peers[i].close != nil {\n\t\t\tctx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(context.Background(), time.Second)\n\t\t\te.Peers[i].close(ctx)\n\t\t\tcancel()\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\tif e.errc != nil {\n\t\te.wg.Wait()\n\t\tclose(e.errc)\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc stopServers(ctx context.Context, ss *servers) {\n\t// first, close the http.Server\n\tif ss.http != nil {\n\t\tss.http.Shutdown(ctx)\n\t}\n\tif ss.grpc == nil {\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\t// do not grpc.Server.GracefulStop when grpc runs under http server\n\t// See https://github.com/grpc/grpc-go/issues/1384#issuecomment-317124531\n\t// and https://github.com/etcd-io/etcd/issues/8916\n\tif ss.secure && ss.http != nil {\n\t\tss.grpc.Stop()\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\tch := make(chan struct{})\n\tgo func() {\n\t\tdefer close(ch)\n\t\t// close listeners to stop accepting new connections,\n\t\t// will block on any existing transports\n\t\tss.grpc.GracefulStop()\n\t}()\n\n\t// wait until all pending RPCs are finished\n\tselect {\n\tcase <-ch:\n\tcase <-ctx.Done():\n\t\t// took too long, manually close open transports\n\t\t// e.g. watch streams\n\t\tss.grpc.Stop()\n\n\t\t// concurrent GracefulStop should be interrupted\n\t\t<-ch\n\t}\n}\n\n// Err - return channel used to report errors during etcd run/shutdown.\n// Since etcd 3.5 the channel is being closed when the etcd is over.\nfunc (e *Etcd) Err() <-chan error {\n\treturn e.errc\n}\n\nfunc configurePeerListeners(cfg *Config) (peers []*peerListener, err error) {\n\tif err = updateCipherSuites(&cfg.PeerTLSInfo, cfg.CipherSuites); err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\tif err = cfg.PeerSelfCert(); err != nil {\n\t\tcfg.logger.Fatal(\"failed to get peer self-signed certs\", zap.Error(err))\n\t}\n\tupdateMinMaxVersions(&cfg.PeerTLSInfo, cfg.TlsMinVersion, cfg.TlsMaxVersion)\n\tif !cfg.PeerTLSInfo.Empty() {\n\t\tcfg.logger.Info(\n\t\t\t\"starting with peer TLS\",\n\t\t\tzap.String(\"tls-info\", fmt.Sprintf(\"%+v\", cfg.PeerTLSInfo)),\n\t\t\tzap.Strings(\"cipher-suites\", cfg.CipherSuites),\n\t\t)\n\t}\n\n\tpeers = make([]*peerListener, len(cfg.ListenPeerUrls))\n\tdefer func() {\n\t\tif err == nil {\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\t\tfor i := range peers {\n\t\t\tif peers[i] != nil && peers[i].close != nil {\n\t\t\t\tcfg.logger.Warn(\n\t\t\t\t\t\"closing peer listener\",\n\t\t\t\t\tzap.String(\"address\", cfg.ListenPeerUrls[i].String()),\n\t\t\t\t\tzap.Error(err),\n\t\t\t\t)\n\t\t\t\tctx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(context.Background(), time.Second)\n\t\t\t\tpeers[i].close(ctx)\n\t\t\t\tcancel()\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}()\n\n\tfor i, u := range cfg.ListenPeerUrls {\n\t\tif u.Scheme == \"http\" {\n\t\t\tif !cfg.PeerTLSInfo.Empty() {\n\t\t\t\tcfg.logger.Warn(\"scheme is HTTP while key and cert files are present; ignoring key and cert files\", zap.String(\"peer-url\", u.String()))\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tif cfg.PeerTLSInfo.ClientCertAuth {\n\t\t\t\tcfg.logger.Warn(\"scheme is HTTP while --peer-client-cert-auth is enabled; ignoring client cert auth for this URL\", zap.String(\"peer-url\", u.String()))\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t\tpeers[i] = &peerListener{close: func(context.Context) error { return nil }}\n\t\tpeers[i].Listener, err = transport.NewListenerWithOpts(u.Host, u.Scheme,\n\t\t\ttransport.WithTLSInfo(&cfg.PeerTLSInfo),\n\t\t\ttransport.WithSocketOpts(&cfg.SocketOpts),\n\t\t\ttransport.WithTimeout(rafthttp.ConnReadTimeout, rafthttp.ConnWriteTimeout),\n\t\t)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\tcfg.logger.Error(\"creating peer listener failed\", zap.Error(err))\n\t\t\treturn nil, err\n\t\t}\n\t\t// once serve, overwrite with 'http.Server.Shutdown'\n\t\tpeers[i].close = func(context.Context) error {\n\t\t\treturn peers[i].Listener.Close()\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn peers, nil\n}\n\n// configure peer handlers after rafthttp.Transport started\nfunc (e *Etcd) servePeers() {\n\tph := etcdhttp.NewPeerHandler(e.GetLogger(), e.Server)\n\n\tfor _, p := range e.Peers {\n\t\tu := p.Listener.Addr().String()\n\t\tm := cmux.New(p.Listener)\n\t\tsrv := &http.Server{\n\t\t\tHandler:     ph,\n\t\t\tReadTimeout: 5 * time.Minute,\n\t\t\tErrorLog:    defaultLog.New(io.Discard, \"\", 0), // do not log user error\n\t\t}\n\t\tgo srv.Serve(m.Match(cmux.Any()))\n\t\tp.serve = func() error {\n\t\t\te.cfg.logger.Info(\n\t\t\t\t\"cmux::serve\",\n\t\t\t\tzap.String(\"address\", u),\n\t\t\t)\n\t\t\treturn m.Serve()\n\t\t}\n\t\tp.close = func(ctx context.Context) error {\n\t\t\t// gracefully shutdown http.Server\n\t\t\t// close open listeners, idle connections\n\t\t\t// until context cancel or time-out\n\t\t\te.cfg.logger.Info(\n\t\t\t\t\"stopping serving peer traffic\",\n\t\t\t\tzap.String(\"address\", u),\n\t\t\t)\n\t\t\tsrv.Shutdown(ctx)\n\t\t\te.cfg.logger.Info(\n\t\t\t\t\"stopped serving peer traffic\",\n\t\t\t\tzap.String(\"address\", u),\n\t\t\t)\n\t\t\tm.Close()\n\t\t\treturn nil\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// start peer servers in a goroutine\n\tfor _, pl := range e.Peers {\n\t\tl := pl\n\t\te.startHandler(func() error {\n\t\t\tu := l.Addr().String()\n\t\t\te.cfg.logger.Info(\n\t\t\t\t\"serving peer traffic\",\n\t\t\t\tzap.String(\"address\", u),\n\t\t\t)\n\t\t\treturn l.serve()\n\t\t})\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc configureClientListeners(cfg *Config) (sctxs map[string]*serveCtx, err error) {\n\tif err = updateCipherSuites(&cfg.ClientTLSInfo, cfg.CipherSuites); err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\tif err = cfg.ClientSelfCert(); err != nil {\n\t\tcfg.logger.Fatal(\"failed to get client self-signed certs\",
